One of the reasons I love this skit so much is that the premise was so absurd and likely would have failed if they had used someone else. This was MADE for Bowen and he knocked it out of the damn park. SNL has its fair share of conceptually random absurdity sketches that, 85% of the time, end in a lot of scratched heads and "ehhh..."s. But god, when those types of skits are executed and acted flawlessly like this -- when the cast member(s) just go all-in, balls-to-the-wall, batshit crazy committed to the bit -- they are PERFECTION. That 15% of the time that they do work is nothing short of magical and this was the cream of the crop, I'm so glad I got to witness this iconic moment of SNL history
This was an absolutely LEGENDARY moment in not just SNL history but television history in general

Honestly if you look into what actually caused the titanic to sink, it's not just the shoddy building work that was done with the second half of the rivets and such on the back side. It's also the fact that they changed one of the main officers at last minute since he had never been in charge of something so large. Since it was changed just as the ship was about to leave port, he had to gether all of his things from around the ship. As he got home he realized that he had left with the key to the closet that housed most if not all of the binoculars on board. Meaning the crows nest had nothing to work with.  So basically cheap craftsmanship on behalf of the company, and the last minute change to the second in command officer who was in such a hurry he forgot to leave the key.  I cant even imagine the way that man felt when he found out why the ship sank...life long guilt im sure.
